I didn't eat in the restaurant. I had eaten Cantonese food there before. There was no disadvantage except that the dishes were slow.
At night, the balcony door couldn't be closed. I called the front desk and someone came to repair it soon. The master was very responsible and it was done in half an hour!
In short, this hotel is very suitable for bringing children. There are food, fun and hot springs.
